width="auto"><div class="stMarkdown" data-testid="stMarkdown"><div data-testid="stMarkdownContainer" class="st-emotion-cache-1104ytp e1icttdg0"><p>UNIT</p>
<p>8</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="digital-logic">DIGITAL LOGIC<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#digital-logic" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="objectives">OBJECTIVES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Digital techniques proved their importance both in electronic computers and electronic communications due to many advantages compared to analog techniques. The basic building blocks of digital circuits are logic gates which can be used in the design and construction of both combinational and sequential logic circuits. Logic gates functions using the principle of non conventional algebra called Boolean algebra. By understanding Boolean algebra and various logic gates which functions using the principle of Boolean algebra, one can design complicated electronic circuits for digital computers and digital communication devices. In this chapter, we will study the Boolean algebra, various logic gates and binary adders using logic gates.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-objectives-are">The objectives are:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-objectives-are" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>(1) To study and understand Boolean algebra and Boolean properties.
(2) To design and analyze Logic gates.
(3) To design and analyze Half-adder, Full-adder, and Parallel Binary adder.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-1-introduction">8.1 INTRODUCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-1-introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="8-1-1-digital-signal">8.1.1 Digital Signal<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-1-1-digital-signal" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>A digital signal is an electrical signal with two levels, (say, 0 volt &amp; 5 volts) or states representing 0 and 1 digits of binary system. It varies between these two levels instantaneously and abruptly depending on the value of the signal. It can be represented in rectangular or square waveform as shown in Fig 8.1.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251224-5b4f3210.jpeg" alt="img-0.jpeg">
Figure 8.1 Representation of digital signal</p>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-1-2-digital-systems">8.1.2 Digital Systems<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-1-2-digital-systems" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>A digital circuit is one in which the voltage levels assume a finite number of distinct values. Digital circuits are often called switching circuits, because the voltage levels in a digital circuit are assumed to be switched from one value to another instantaneously, that is, the transition time is assumed to be zero. Digital circuits are also called logic circuits, because each type of digital circuit obeys a certain set of logic rules. Digital systems are used extensively in computation and data processing, control systems, communications and measurement.</p>
<p>Digital systems have a number of advantages over analog systems. Many tasks formally done by analog systems are now being performed digitally. The main reasons for the shift to digital technology are given below:</p>
<p>(i) Digital systems are easier to design: The switching circuits in which there are only two voltage levels, HIGH and LOW, are easier to design. The exact numerical values of voltages are not important because they have only logical significance; only the range in which they fall is important. In analog systems, signals have numerical significance; so, their design is more complex.</p>
<p>(ii) Information storage is easy: There are many types of semiconductor and magnetic memories of large capacity which can store data for long periods.</p>
<p>(iii) Accuracy and precision are greater: Digital systems are much more accurate and precise than analog systems, because digital systems can be easily expanded to handle more digits by adding more switching circuits. Analog systems will be quite complex and costly for the same accuracy and precision.</p>
<p>(iv) Digital systems are more versatile: It is fairly easy to design digital systems whose operation is controlled by a set of stored instructions called the program. Any time the system operation is to be changed, it can easily be accomplished by modifying the program. Even though analog systems can also be programmed, the variety of the available operations is severely limited.</p>
<p>(v) Digital circuits are less affected by noise: Unwanted electrical signals are called noise. In analog systems the exact values of voltages are important and in digital systems only the range of values is important. The effect of noise is more severe in analog systems. In digital systems, noise is not critical as long as it is not large enough to prevent us from distinguishing a HIGH from a LOW.</p>
<p>(vi) More digital circuitry can be fabricated on IC chips: The fabrication of digital ICs is simpler and economical than that of analog ICs. Moreover, higher densities of integration can be achieved in digital ICs than in analog ICs, because digital design does not require high value capacitors, precision resistors, inductors and transformers (which cannot be integrated economically) like the analog design.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="limitations-of-digital-techniques">Limitations of digital techniques:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#limitations-of-digital-techniques" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Even though digital techniques have a number of advantages, they have only one major drawback. THE REAL WORLD IS ANALOG. Most physical quantities are analog in nature, and it is these quantities that are often the inputs and outputs and continually monitored, operated and controlled by a system. When these, quantities are processed and expressed digitally, we are really making a digital approximation to an analog quantity. Instead of processing the analog information directly, it is first converted into digital form and then processed using digital techniques. The results of processing can be converted</p>
<p>Digital Logic</p>
<p>back to analog form for interpretation. Because of these conversions, the processing time increases and the system becomes more complex. In most cases, these disadvantages are outweighed by numerous advantages of digital techniques. However, there are situations where using only analog techniques is simpler and more economical. Both the analog and digital techniques can be employed in the same system to advantage. Such systems are called hybrid systems. But the tendency today is towards employing digital systems because the economic benefits of integration are of overriding importance.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-1-3-logic-levels">8.1.3 Logic Levels<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-1-3-logic-levels" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Digital systems use the binary number system. Therefore, two-state devices are used to represent the two binary digits 1 and 0 by two different voltage levels, called HIGH and LOW. If the HIGH voltage level is used to represent 1 and the LOW voltage level is used to represent 0, the system is called the positive logic system. On the other hand, if the HIGH voltage level represents 0 and the LOW voltage level represents 1, the system is called the negative logic system.</p>
<p>Normally, the binary 0 and 1 are represented by the logic voltage levels <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">+5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>. So, in a positive logic system, 1 is represented by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">+5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> (HIGH) and 0 is represented by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> (LOW); and in a negative logic system, 0 is represented by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>5</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">+5\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">+</span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> (HIGH) and 1 is represented by <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> (LOW). Both positive and negative logics are used in digital systems, but the positive logic is more common.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-boolean-algebra">8.2 BOOLEAN ALGEBRA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-boolean-algebra" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Boolean algebra is a kind of logical mathematics developed by George Boole in the late 1830s. It resembles the algebra of real numbers but the basic numeric operations of multiplication, addition, and negation are replaced by basic logical operations of conjunction, disjunction, and complement and are also called OR operation, AND operation and NOT operation respectively. These basic local operators are used to represent and reduce all mathematics of logical expressions in Boolean algebra. Boolean algebra is also known as 'Laws of Thoughts' which codified several rules of relationship between mathematical quantities limited to one of two possible values: true or false, 1 or 0.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-1-boolean-arithmetic">8.2.1 Boolean Arithmetic<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-1-boolean-arithmetic" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>All arithmetic operations performed with Boolean quantities gives one of two possible outcomes: either 1 or 0. The Boolean arithmetic using OR, AND, and NOT logical operations are discussed below:</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="or-logical-operation">OR Logical Operation:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#or-logical-operation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>The Boolean arithmetic using OR logical operation is given below and is called Truth Table of OR logical operation. The equivalent logical symbol is also given.</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>0 + 0 = 0</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>0 + 1 = 1</td></tr><tr><td>1 + 0 = 1</td></tr><tr><td>1 + 1 = 1</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Truth Table of OR logical operation</p>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>OR Operation</th><th>OR gate equivalent Symbol</th><th>Parallel switch equivalent</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>0 + 0 = 0</td><td>0 0</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>0 + 1 = 1</td><td>0 1</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>1 + 0 = 1</td><td>1 0</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>1 + 1 = 1</td><td>1 1</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Boolean addition is equivalent to the OR logic operation as well as parallel switch contacts.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="and-logical-operation">AND Logical Operation:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#and-logical-operation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The Boolean arithmetic using AND logical operation is given below and is called Truth Table of AND logical operation. The equivalent logical symbol is also given.</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>0 . 0 = 0</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>0 . 1 = 0</td></tr><tr><td>1 . 0 = 0</td></tr><tr><td>1 . 1 = 1</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Truth Table of AND logical operation</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>AND Operation</th><th>AND gate equivalent Symbol</th><th>Series switch equivalent</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>0.0=0</td><td>0 0</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>0.1=0</td><td>0 1</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>1.0=0</td><td>1 0</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr><tr><td>1.1=1</td><td>1 1</td><td>0 S1 S2</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Digital Logic</p>
<p>Boolean multiplication is equivalent to the AND logic operation as well as series switch contacts.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="not-logical-operation">NOT Logical Operation:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#not-logical-operation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>

0.35em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Boolean complementation is equivalent to the NOT logic operation. In NOT operation, output is always complement of the input and hence it is called complement operation.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-2-boolean-identities">8.2.2 Boolean Identities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-2-boolean-identities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>In mathematics, an identity is a statement which is true for all possible values of its variable. The algebraic identity <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + 0 = A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span></span> tells us that anything (A) added to zero equals the original anything, no matter what value that anything may be. Accordingly we can write basic Boolean Identities as follows:</p>
<p>Basic Boolean Algebraic Identities</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Additive</th><th>Multiplicative</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + 0 = A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord <div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-3-properties-of-boolean-algebra">8.2.3 Properties of Boolean Algebra<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-3-properties-of-boolean-algebra" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Another type of mathematical identity called "Property" or "Law" describes how different variables relate to each other in a system of numbers. These properties are mostly applicable equally to addition and multiplication. The properties applicable to Boolean Algebra are given below:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Associative Law
(A.B).C = A.(B.C) = A.B.C
(A + B) + C = A + (B + C) = A + B + C</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Commutative Law
A . B = B . A
A + B = B + A</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Distributive Law
A.(B+C) = (A.B) + (A.C)
A+(B.C) = (A+B) . (A+C)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Precedence
AB = A.B
A.B+C = (A.B) + C
A+B.C = A + (B.C)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<p>The combinational symbolic equivalent of Associative property of Addition and Multiplication are shown in following Tables:</p>
<p>Table 8.3 Associative property for addition:  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A} + \left( {\mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C}}\right)  = \left( {\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{B}}\right)  + \mathrm{C}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Symbolic Equivalent</th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>A B C</td><td>A+B (C)</td><td>(A+B) + C=</td><td>B C</td><td>B+C A</td><td>A+(B+C)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>A</td><td>B</td><td>C</td><td>A+B</td><td>(A+B)+C</td><td>A</td><td>B</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>This law can be extended to any number of variables. For example,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm {A} + (\mathrm {B} + \mathrm {C} + \mathrm {D}) = (\mathrm {A} + \mathrm {B} + \mathrm {C}) + \mathrm {D} = (\mathrm {A} + \mathrm {B}) + (\mathrm {C} + \mathrm {D}).</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <table><thead><tr><th>Symbolic Equivalent</th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>A B C</td><td>AB (A)C</td><td>(AB)C</td><td>B C</td><td>BC A</td><td>A(BC)</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>A</td><td>B</td><td>C</td><td>AB</td><td>(AB)C</td><td>A</td><td>B</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>This law can be extended to any number of variables. For example,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm {A} (\mathrm {B C D}) = (\mathrm {A B C}) \mathrm {D} = (\mathrm {A B}) (\mathrm {C D})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p>This law applies to single variables as well as combinations of variables. For example,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>E</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mi>E</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A B C (D + E) = A B C D + A B C E</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>E</mi><mi>F</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>E</mi><mi>F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A B (C D + E F) = A B C D + A B E F</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p>Table 8.8 Distributive property for multiplication:  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A} + \left( {\mathrm{B} \cdot  \mathrm{C}}\right)  = \left( {\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{B}}\right) ,\left( {\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{C}}\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Symbolic Equivalent</th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>C B A B C B AC A+BC</td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td>A+B B A A+C A+B A+C A+B A+C A+B A+C A+B A+C A+B A+C</td></tr><tr><td>A</td><td>B</td><td>C</td><td>BC</td><td>A+BC</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td></td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>1</td><td></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Digital Logic</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-4-boolean-rules-for-simplification">8.2.4 Boolean Rules for Simplification<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-4-boolean-rules-for-simplification" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The following rules are used for simplification of Boolean expressions:</p>
<p>(1)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{AB} = \mathrm{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AB</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span></span></span>  ... (8.1)</p>
<p>Proof:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + AB = A (1 + B) = A (1) = A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>(2)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A(A + B) = A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span></span></span></span>  ... (8.2)</p>
<p>Proof:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mn>.1</mn><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A (A + B) = AA + AB = A + AB = A (1 + B) = A. 1 = A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">AA</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord">.1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>(3)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A} + \overline{\mathrm{A}}\mathrm{B} = \mathrm{A} + \mathrm{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span></span></span></span></span>  ... (8.3)</p>
<p>Proof:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo>ˉ</mo></mover><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo>ˉ</mo></mover><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo>ˉ</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + \bar {A} B = A + AB + \bar {A} B = A + B (A + \bar {A}) = A + B (1) = A + B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8201em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8201em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span><span style="top: -3.2523em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.1111em;"><span class="mord">ˉ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8201em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8201em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span><span style="top: -3.2523em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.1111em;"><span class="mord">ˉ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0701em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8201em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span><span style="top: -3.2523em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.1111em;"><span class="mord">ˉ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>(4)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{B})(\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{C}) = \mathrm{A} + \mathrm{BC}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BC</span></span></span></span></span></span>  ... (8.4)</p>
<p>Proof:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathrm {A} + \mathrm {B}) (\mathrm {A} + \mathrm {C}) = \mathrm {A A} + \mathrm {A C} + \mathrm {A B} + \mathrm {B C} = \mathrm {A} + \mathrm {A C} + \mathrm {A B} + \mathrm {B C} = \mathrm {A} + \mathrm {A B} + \mathrm {B C} = \mathrm {A} + \mathrm {B C}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p>(ii)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{B}(\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{C}) + \mathrm{AC}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">C</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AC</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>Distributing&nbsp;terms</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{c}
\text{Distributing terms} \\
\mathrm{A} + \mathrm{AB} + \mathrm{BC} + \mathrm{AC}
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.4em; vertical-align: -0.95em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-c"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.45em;"><span style="top: -3.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Distributing&nbsp;terms</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -2.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AB</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BC</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AC</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.95em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>↓</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\downarrow</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mrel">↓</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>Using&nbsp;rule</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{c}

<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mtext>Using&nbsp;rule</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{c}

<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<p>Example 2: Prove the Boolean identity: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(A + B)(A + C) = A + BC</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">BC</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
Y = (A + B)(A + C) \\
= AA + AC + AB + BC \\
= A + AC + AB + BC \\
= A + AB + AC + BC = A(1 + B) + AC + BC \\
= A + AC + BC \\
= A(1 + C) + BC = A + BC \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 7.2em; vertical-align: -3.35em;"></span><span <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>∴</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\therefore \quad (A + B)(A + C) = A + BC</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">∴</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">BC</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Example 3: Prove the Boolean identity: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + \overline{A}B = A + B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mn>.1</mn><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>B</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>B</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mn>.1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>B</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mn>.1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
Y = A + \overline{A}B = A.1 + \overline{A}B \\
= A(1 + B) + \overline{A}B \\
= A.1 + AB + \overline{A}B \\
= A + BA + B \overline{A} \\
= A + B(A + \overline{A}) \\
= A + B.1 \\
= A + B \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 8.6166em; vertical-align: -4.0583em;"></span><span style="height: 4.5583em;"><span style="top: -6.675em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace"
