class="vlist" style="height: 4.0583em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo>∴</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo>^</mo></mover><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\therefore \quad A + \hat{A}B = A + B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6922em;"></span><span class="mrel amsrm">∴</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9468em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9468em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span><span style="top: -3.2523em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.1111em;"><span class="mord">^</span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="8-2-5-de-morgan-s-theorems">8.2.5 De-Morgan's Theorems<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#8-2-5-de-morgan-s-theorems" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>A mathematician named De-Morgan developed two important rules related to the group complementation in Boolean Algebra.</p>
<p>De-Morgan's Theorem 1: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{A \cdot B} = \overline{A} + \overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  (NAND function) ...(8.5)</p>
<p>De-Morgan's Theorem 2: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>⋅</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{A + B} = \overline{A} \cdot \overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.0833em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  (NOR function) ...(8.6)</p>
<p>De-Morgan's theorems can be used to break long bars in Boolean expressions. While breaking a long bar, the operation directly under the break changes from addition to multiplication or vice-versa and broken bar pieces remain over individual variables.</p>
<p>(i) Proof of De-Morgan's Theorem 1: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{A \cdot B} = \overline{A} + \overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>:</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251224-6aa2be8c.jpeg" alt="img-1.jpeg"></p>
<p>Digital Logic</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251224-a1821357.jpeg" alt="img-2.jpeg">
RHS</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>A</th><th>B</th><th>A̅B</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>A</td><td>B</td><td>A̅</td></tr><tr><td>---</td><td>---</td><td>---</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>1</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>0</td><td>0</td></tr><tr><td>1</td><td>1</td><td>0</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>It shows that the NAND gate is equivalent to a bubbled OR gate.</p>
<p>This law can be extended to any number of variables or combinations of variables. For example,</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>⋯</mo><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mo>…</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline {{\mathrm {A B C D}}} \dots = \overline {{\mathrm {A}}} + \overline {{\mathrm {B}}} + \overline {{\mathrm {C}}} + \overline {{\mathrm {D}}} + \dots</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">ABCD</span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">⋯</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; <p>Example 4: Simplifications of Boolean expressions using De-Morgan's Theorem</p>
<p>(i)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>⋅</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathrm{A} + \overline{\mathrm{B}}\cdot\overline{\mathrm{C}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.1667em; <p>Breaking longest bar (Addition changes Multiplication)</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi <p>Applying identity  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\overline{\mathrm{A}}} = \mathrm{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -4.0033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathrm{A}}.\overline{\mathrm{BC}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BC</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(ii)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathrm{A} + \overline{\mathrm{BC}}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.1667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BC</span></span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -4.0033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.0833em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  Method II</p>
<p>Breaking shortest bar first (Multiplication changes to Addition)</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\mathrm{A} + (\overline{\mathrm{B}} + \overline{\mathrm{C}})}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.3333em; <p>Breaking bar in two place</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi <p>Applying  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{\overline{\mathrm{A}}} = \mathrm{A}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.0833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -4.0033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi <p>A  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(v) Apply De-morgan's theorem to the expression</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>E</mi><mi>F</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{AB} (CD + \overline{EF}) (\overline{AB} + \overline{CD})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.1333em; <p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<p>The given expression is</p>

accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mover = \overline{AB} (CD + \overline{EF}) (\overline{AB} + \overline{CD}) \\
= \overline{AB} + \overline{CD} + \overline{EF} + (\overline{AB} + \overline{CD}) \\
= AB + (\overline{CD} \cdot \overline{EF}) + (\overline{AB} \cdot \overline{CD}) \\
= AB + (\overline{C} + \overline{D}) (E + \overline{F}) + ABCD \\

<p><strong>Example 5:</strong> Reduce the expression</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + B [AC + (B + \overline{C})D]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.1333em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mi>D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>D</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
A + B [AC + (B + \overline{C})D] \\
= A + B (AC + BD + \overline{CD}) \\
= A + BAC + BBD + \overline{BCD} \\
= A + ABC + BD + BD\overline{C} \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 4.9733em; vertical-align: -2.2367em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.7367em;"><span style="top: -4.8533em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">C</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mspace" 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: <p>Basic Electronics</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow><mo>⋅</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
= \mathrm{A}(1 + \mathrm{BC}) + \mathrm{BD}(1 + \overline{\mathrm{C}}) \\
= \mathrm{A} \cdot 1 + \mathrm{BD} \cdot 1 \\
= \mathrm{A} + \mathrm{BD}
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.6433em; vertical-align: -1.5717em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.0717em;"><span style="top: -4.1883em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">A</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BC</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BD</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BD</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span><span style="top: -1.7883em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">BD</span></span></span></span></span><span
