<p>(iii) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>A</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0(A_2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0(B_2)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> and CARRY 1 are the inputs to the third full adder</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;and&nbsp;CARRY&nbsp;0&nbsp;is&nbsp;generated</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0 + 0 + 1 = 1 = S_2 \text{ and CARRY 0 is generated}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;and&nbsp;CARRY&nbsp;0&nbsp;is&nbsp;generated</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>(iv) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>A</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1(A_3)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>B</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1(B_3)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> and a CARRY 0 are the inputs to the final full adder.</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mtext>&nbsp;and&nbsp;a&nbsp;CARRY&nbsp;</mtext><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mtext>&nbsp;is&nbsp;generated</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1 + 1 + 0 = 0 = S_3 \text{ and a CARRY } 1(S_4) \text{ is generated}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;and&nbsp;a&nbsp;CARRY&nbsp;</span></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">4</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">&nbsp;is&nbsp;generated</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Hence the final output is</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="center center center center" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn></msub></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><msub><mi>S</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mn>1</mn></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{cccc}
S_4 &amp;amp; S_3 &amp;amp; S_2 &amp;amp; S_1 &amp;amp; S_0 \\
1 &amp;amp; 0 &amp;amp; 1 &amp;amp; 0 &amp;amp; 0
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 2.4em; vertical-align: -0.95em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-c"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.45em;"><span style="top: -3.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">S</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo X = A \overline{B} + \overline{A} B \\
= A \overline{A} + A \overline{B} + \overline{A} B + B \overline{B} \\
= A (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) + B (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) \\
= A \overline{A B} + B \overline{A B} \\
= \overline{A \overline{A B} + B \overline{A B}} \\
= \overline{A \overline{A B}} \cdot \overline{B \overline{A B}} \\

encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
X = A \overline{B} + \overline{A} B \\
= A \overline{A} + A \overline{B} + \overline{A} B + B \overline{B} \\
= A (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) + B (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) \\
= (A + B) (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) \\
= \overline{(A + B) (\overline{A} + \overline{B})} \\
= \overline{(\overline{A} + \overline{B}) + (\overline{A} + \overline{B})} \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 7.86em; vertical-align: -3.68em;"></span><span displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
= A \left[ B + \overline{C} (\overline{A} \overline{B} \overline{A} \overline{C}) \right] \\
= A \left[ B + \overline{C} (\overline{A} + \overline{B}) (\overline{A} + C) \right] \\
= A \left[ B + \overline{C} (\overline{A} \overline{A} + \overline{A} C + \overline{B} \overline{A} + \overline{B} C) \right] \\
= A \left( B + \overline{C} \overline{A} + \overline{C} \overline{A} C + \overline{C} \overline{B} \overline{A} + \overline{C} \overline{B} C \right) \\
= A \left( B + \overline{C} \overline{A} + 0 + \overline{C} \overline{B} \overline{A} + 0 \right) \\
= A B + A \overline{C} \overline{A} + A \overline{C} \overline{B} \overline{A} \\
= A B + 0 + 0 \\
= A B \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 9.86em; vertical-align: -4.68em;"></span><span A + B [AC + (B + \overline{C})D] \\
= A + B (AC + BD + \overline{C}D) \\
= A + BAC + BBD + B \overline{C}D \\
= A + ABC + BD + BD \overline{C} \\
= A (1 + BC) + BD (1 + \overline{C}) \\
= A \cdot 1 + BD \cdot 1 \\
= A + BD \\

<p>Digital Logic</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable = (\overline{A} \overline{B C}) (A \overline{B} + A B C) \\
= (\overline{A} B C) (A \overline{B} + A B C) \\

<ol start="5">
<li>Reduce the expression</li>
</ol>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(B + B C) (B + \overline{B} C) (B + D)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p>Solution:</p>
<p>The given expression is</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable (B + B C) (B + \overline{B} C) (B + D) \\
= (B B + B C B + B \overline{B} C + B C \overline{B} C) (B + D) \\
= (B + B C + 0 + 0) (B + D) \\
= B (1 + C) (B + D) \\
= B (B + D) \\
= B B + B D \\
= B (1 + D) = B \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 8.4867em; vertical-align: -3.9933em;"></span><span <ol start="6">
<li>Show that</li>
</ol>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A B + A \overline{B} C + B \overline{C} = A C + B \overline{C}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; <p>Solution:</p>
<p>The given expression is</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>C</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi>C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
A B + A \overline{B} C + B \overline{C} = A (B + \overline{B} C) + B \overline{C} \\
= A (B + \overline{B}) (B + C) + B \overline{C} \\
= A B + A C + B \overline{C} \\
= A B (C + \overline{C}) + A C + B \overline{C} \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 4.9733em; vertical-align: -2.2367em;"></span><span <p>Basic Electronics</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.16em" columnalign="left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
= \mathrm{ABC} + \mathrm{AB}\overline{\mathrm{C}} + \mathrm{AC} + \mathrm{B}\overline{\mathrm{C}} \\
= \mathrm{AC}(1 + \mathrm{B}) + \mathrm{B}\overline{\mathrm{C}}(1 + \mathrm{A}) \\
= \mathrm{AC} + \mathrm{B}\overline{\mathrm{C}} \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 3.73em; vertical-align: -1.615em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.115em;"><span style="top: -4.2317em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">ABC</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AB</span></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AC</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">C</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top: -2.9883em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">AC</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span <ol start="7">
<li>Show that</li>
</ol>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{A}\overline{\mathrm{BC}} + \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{B}\overline{\mathrm{D}} + \mathrm{AB}\overline{\mathrm{D}} + \overline{\mathrm{AC}} = \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; <p>Solution:</p>
<p>The given expression is</p>

scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">C</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{array}{l}
\mathrm{A}\overline{\mathrm{BC}} + \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{B}\overline{\mathrm{D}} + \mathrm{AB}\overline{\mathrm{D}} + \overline{\mathrm{AC}} \\
= \mathrm{A}\overline{\mathrm{BC}} + \overline{\mathrm{AC}} + \mathrm{B}(1 + \overline{\mathrm{D}} + \mathrm{A}\overline{\mathrm{D}}) \\
= \mathrm{C}(\overline{\mathrm{A}} + \mathrm{A}\overline{\mathrm{B}}) + \mathrm{B} \\
= \mathrm{C}(\overline{\mathrm{A}} + \mathrm{A})(\overline{\mathrm{A}} + \overline{\mathrm{B}}) + \mathrm{B} \\
= \mathrm{C}\overline{\mathrm{A}} + \mathrm{C}\overline{\mathrm{B}} + \mathrm{B} \\
= (\mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C})(\mathrm{B} + \overline{\mathrm{B}}) + \mathrm{C}\overline{\mathrm{A}} \\
= \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C} + \mathrm{C}\overline{\mathrm{A}} \\
= \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C}(1 + \overline{\mathrm{A}}) \\
= \mathrm{B} + \mathrm{C} \\
\end{array}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 11.1466em; vertical-align: -5.3233em;"></span><span <p>Digital Logic</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="exercises">EXERCISES<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#exercises" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="i-descriptive-type-questions">I. Descriptive Type Questions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#i-descriptive-type-questions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>Write the truth table of an OR function and realize an OR gate using diodes.</li>
<li>Simplify and realize the following using NAND gates A B C + A B C + A B + A C.</li>
<li>Realize a half adder using AND, OR and inverter logic gates. Write the truth table.</li>
<li>Realize a full adder using two half adders.</li>
<li>Draw the logic circuit for Full Adder and write its truth table.</li>
<li>Explain how AND, OR and NOT gates can be obtained using only NOR gates.</li>
<li>Realize full adder using two half adders and OR gate.</li>
<li>Realize AND gate using diodes.</li>
<li>Implement XNOR using only NOR gate.</li>
<li>List the properties of Boolean Algebra with an example.</li>
<li>Draw a full adder circuit with the truth table.</li>
<li>Implement OR and AND gates using NOR gates.</li>
<li>Realize full adder using (i) NAND gates and (ii) NOR gates</li>
<li>Realize half adder using (i) NAND gates and (ii) NOR gates</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="ii-multiple-choice-questions">II. Multiple Choice Questions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#ii-multiple-choice-questions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ol>
<li>
<p>The Boolean expression <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>A</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y = A.B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> represents ________
(a) OR gate
(b) XNOR gate
(c) AND gate
(d) NOT gate</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>To add two m-bit number, the number of required half adders is ________
(a) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>m</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2m - 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>
(b) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>m</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2m</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span></span></span></span></span>
(c) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>m</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2m - 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>
(d) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>m</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2m + 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<ol start="5">
<li>De-Morgan theorem states that <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + B =</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span></span></span></span> _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{A} + \overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(b) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>⋅</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{A} \cdot \overline{B}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(c) <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{AB}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8833em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8033em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(d) None</p>
<ol start="6">
<li>Universal gates are _______________ and _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) NOT and NOR</p>
<p>(b) AND and OR</p>
<p>(c) NAND and NOR</p>
<p>(d) EXOR and EX-NOR</p>
<ol start="7">
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>=</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + AB + A =</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span></span></span></span> _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) AB</p>
<p>(c) A + B</p>
<p>(c) A</p>
<p>(d) 0</p>
<ol start="8">
<li>The output is High only when all the inputs are high, such a gate is called.</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) NAND</p>
<p>(b) NOR</p>
<p>(c) AND</p>
<p>(d) OR</p>
<ol start="9">
<li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>A</mi><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A + AB =</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span></span></span></span> _______________</li>

<p>(a) AB</p>
<p>(b) A</p>
<p>(c) B</p>
<p>(d) 1+A</p>

<li>Universal gate is _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) NOT</p>
<p>(b) AND</p>
<p>(c) OR</p>
<p>(d) NAND</p>
<ol start="11">
<li>If <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x + 1 = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>⋅</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \cdot 1 = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>, then <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span></span></span></span></span> is _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) 0</p>
<p>(b) 1</p>
<p>(c) Could be 0 or 1</p>
<p>(d) Situation can never be true</p>
<ol start="12">
<li>The output is high only when both inputs are zero to a gate. The gate is _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) AND</p>
<p>(b) NOR</p>
<p>(c) OR</p>
<p>(d) NAND.</p>
<ol start="13">
<li>A logic gate is an electronic circuit which _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) makes logic decisions</p>
<p>(b) allows electron flow only in one direction</p>
<p>(c) works on binary algebra</p>
<p>(d) alternates between 0 and 1 values</p>
<ol start="14">
<li>In positive logic, logic state 1 corresponds to _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) positive voltage</p>
<p>(b) higher voltage level</p>
<p>(c) zero voltage level</p>
<p>(d) lower voltage level</p>
<ol start="15">
<li>In negative logic, logic state 1 corresponds to _______________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) negative voltage</p>
<p>(b) zero voltage</p>
<p>(c) more negative voltage</p>
<p>(d) lower voltage level</p>
<p>Digital Logic</p>
<ol start="16">

</ol>
<p>(a) both inputs are 0</p>
<p>(b) either input is 1</p>
<p>(c) both inputs are 1</p>
<p>(d) either input is 0</p>

</ol>
<p>(a) high</p>
<p>(b) low</p>
<p>(c) different</p>
<p>(d) same</p>
<ol start="18">

</ol>
<p>(a) implements logic addition</p>
<p>(b) is equivalent to a series switching circuit</p>
<p>(c) is an any-or-all gate</p>
<p>(d) is equivalent to a parallel switching circuit</p>

<p>(b) 10101</p>

<p>(d) 00101</p>
<ol start="20">
<li>The only function of a NOT gate is to ________</li>
</ol>
<p>(a) stop a signal</p>
<p>(b) recomplement a signal</p>
<p>(c) invert an input signal</p>
<p>(d) act as a universal gate</p>
<ol start="21">

</ol>
<p>(a) ON</p>
<p>(b) positive</p>
<p>(c) high</p>
<p>(d) OFF</p>
<ol start="22">

<ol start="2">
<li>Realize the following expressions using only NAND gates.</li>
</ol>
<p>(i)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>b</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{Y} = \overline{ab} + \overline{ab}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.025em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.9778em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8944em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ab</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8144em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8944em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8944em;"><span style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ab</span></span></span><span style="top: -3.8144em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>(ii)  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo>+</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo>⋅</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>A</mi><mo stretchy="true">‾</mo></mover><mo>+</mo><mi>B</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>C</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{Y} = \left( A + \overline{B} + C \right) \cdot \left( \overline{A} + B + C \right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.025em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.2333em;
